# Experimental Results

## Control Group

### Partition 1
- **Model**: Standard model with fixed 1024x1024 resolution and weighted loss function
  - Resolution: 1024
  - Class balancing: weighted_loss
  - Anatomical adaptation: none

## Experimental Group

### Partition 1
- **Model 1**: Model with multi-scale approach using both 512x512 and 1024x1024 resolutions
  - Resolution: 512
  - Class balancing: weighted_loss
  - Anatomical adaptation: none

- **Model 2**: Model with anatomical site-specific branches that specialize in different body locations
  - Resolution: 1024
  - Class balancing: weighted_loss
  - Anatomical adaptation: site_specific_branches

These results represent the experimental plan for examining the hypothesis that multi-resolution approaches and anatomical site-specific model adaptations will improve melanoma classification performance. The experiment compares a standard 1024x1024 resolution model (control) against two experimental approaches: a multi-scale model using both 512x512 and 1024x1024 resolutions, and a model with anatomical site-specific branches.

The experiment is set up to measure the effect on AUC-ROC scores, recall for the minority class, and computational efficiency while keeping constant the base model architecture, metadata features, data augmentation strategy, and evaluation protocol.

Note: The raw experiment results have not been included in the provided information, so actual performance metrics cannot be reported.
# Experimental Results: Skin Lesion Melanoma Prediction

## Experiment Setup
- **Question**: Develop a machine learning model to predict the probability that a skin lesion image is malignant (melanoma), with the goal of maximizing the AUC-ROC on the test set.
- **Hypothesis**: A deep convolutional neural network with image augmentation and metadata integration will outperform a baseline CNN model without metadata in predicting melanoma probability.

## Control Group Results
**Model**: baseline_resnet50
- **Configuration**:
  - Use metadata: False
  - Image augmentation: Basic (flips, rotations)
  - Description: ResNet50 CNN trained on images only with basic augmentation

**Dataset Split**:
- Train set: 2,636 samples (2,636 patients)
- Validation set: 329 samples (329 patients)
- Test set: 330 samples (330 patients)

**Training Performance**:
- Epoch 1/2 | Train Loss: 0.2862 | Val Loss: 0.1565 | Val AUC: 0.9895
- Epoch 2/2 | Train Loss: 0.1827 | Val Loss: 0.1835 | Val AUC: 0.9903

**Test Metrics**:
- AUC-ROC: 0.9836
- Accuracy: 0.9152
- Precision: 0.9216
- Recall: 0.9152
- F1 Score: 0.9150

## Experimental Group Status

1. ResNet50 with concatenated metadata features before final classification layers
2. EfficientNetB3 with metadata integration and advanced augmentation (including color jittering, cutout, etc.)

# Experiment Results Extraction

## Experiment Plan Overview
This experiment aimed to evaluate the best-performing melanoma prediction model's real-world applicability through:
1. External validation testing
2. Performance assessment on difficult cases
3. Probability calibration evaluation

The hypothesis was that while the model might achieve high AUC-ROC on the main validation set, it could show weaknesses with external validation data, require probability calibration, and struggle with difficult clinical edge cases.

- **Partition 1**: Best performing model from previous experiments with standard probability outputs

  - Calibration: None

     - Difficult case focus: No
     - Calibration: None

     - External validation: No

# Python Code Snippets for Melanoma Classification Models

## Standard Approach (Control Group)

```python
class StandardMelanomaClassifier(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, num_metadata_features=3):
        super().__init__()
        # Image feature extractor
        self.efficientnet = EfficientNet.from_pretrained('efficientnet-b4')
        self.image_features_dim = self.efficientnet._fc.in_features
        self.efficientnet._fc = nn.Identity()
        
        # Metadata processing
        self.metadata_encoder = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Linear(num_metadata_features, 64),
            nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Linear(64, 128)
        )
        
        # Classifier head with concatenated features
        self.classifier = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Linear(self.image_features_dim + 128, 512),
            nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Dropout(0.3),
            nn.Linear(512, 1)
        )
        
    def forward(self, images, metadata):
        # Extract image features
        image_features = self.efficientnet(images)
        
        # Process metadata
        metadata_features = self.metadata_encoder(metadata)
        
        # Concatenate features
        combined_features = torch.cat([image_features, metadata_features], dim=1)
        
        # Classification
        output = self.classifier(combined_features)
        return output
```

## Self-Attention Approach (Experimental Group #1)

```python
class SelfAttentionMelanomaClassifier(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, num_metadata_features=3):
        super().__init__()
        # Image feature extractor
        self.efficientnet = EfficientNet.from_pretrained('efficientnet-b4')
        self.image_features_dim = self.efficientnet._fc.in_features
        self.efficientnet._fc = nn.Identity()
        
        # Spatial self-attention for lesion area focus
        self.self_attention = nn.MultiheadAttention(
            embed_dim=self.image_features_dim, 
            num_heads=8,
            dropout=0.1
        )
        
        # Metadata processing
        self.metadata_encoder = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Linear(num_metadata_features, 64),
            nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Linear(64, 128)
        )
        
        # Classifier head
        self.classifier = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Linear(self.image_features_dim + 128, 512),
            nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Dropout(0.3),
            nn.Linear(512, 1)
        )
        
    def forward(self, images, metadata):
        # Extract image features
        image_features = self.efficientnet(images)
        
        # Apply self-attention to focus on lesion areas
        # Reshape for attention (seq_len, batch, features)
        image_features_reshaped = image_features.unsqueeze(0)
        attended_features, _ = self.self_attention(
            image_features_reshaped, 
            image_features_reshaped, 
            image_features_reshaped
        )
        attended_features = attended_features.squeeze(0)
        
        # Process metadata
        metadata_features = self.metadata_encoder(metadata)
        
        # Concatenate features
        combined_features = torch.cat([attended_features, metadata_features], dim=1)
        
        # Classification
        output = self.classifier(combined_features)
        return output
```

## Cross-Attention Approach (Experimental Group #2)

```python
class CrossAttentionMelanomaClassifier(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, num_metadata_features=3):
        super().__init__()
        # Image feature extractor
        self.efficientnet = EfficientNet.from_pretrained('efficientnet-b4')
        self.image_features_dim = self.efficientnet._fc.in_features
        self.efficientnet._fc = nn.Identity()
        
        # Metadata processing
        self.metadata_encoder = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Linear(num_metadata_features, 64),
            nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Linear(64, self.image_features_dim)
        )
        
        # Cross-attention between image features and metadata
        self.cross_attention = nn.MultiheadAttention(
            embed_dim=self.image_features_dim, 
            num_heads=8,
            dropout=0.1
        )
        
        # Classifier head
        self.classifier = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Linear(self.image_features_dim, 512),
            nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Dropout(0.3),
            nn.Linear(512, 1)
        )
        
    def forward(self, images, metadata):
        # Extract image features
        image_features = self.efficientnet(images)
        
        # Process metadata
        metadata_features = self.metadata_encoder(metadata)
        
        # Apply cross-attention between image features and metadata
        # Reshaping for attention dimensions (seq_len, batch, features)
        image_features_reshaped = image_features.unsqueeze(0)
        metadata_features_reshaped = metadata_features.unsqueeze(0)
        
        # Use image features as queries and metadata as keys/values
        attended_features, _ = self.cross_attention(
            query=image_features_reshaped,
            key=metadata_features_reshaped,
            value=metadata_features_reshaped
        )
        attended_features = attended_features.squeeze(0)
        
        # Classification
        output = self.classifier(attended_features)
        return output
```

The key differences between these approaches:

1. **Standard Approach**: Simple concatenation of image and metadata features before classification

2. **Self-Attention Approach**: Applies self-attention to image features to focus on important regions of the skin lesion before combining with metadata

3. **Cross-Attention Approach**: Uses cross-attention to create explicit relationships between image features and metadata, allowing the model to attend to image regions relevant to the metadata

Running `shell init`, which:

 - modifies RC file: "/root/.bashrc"

 - generates config for root prefix: [1m"/root/.local/share/mamba"[0m

 - sets mamba executable to: [1m"/usr/local/bin/micromamba"[0m

The following has been added in your "/root/.bashrc" file



# >>> mamba initialize >>>

# !! Contents within this block are managed by 'micromamba shell init' !!

export MAMBA_EXE='/usr/local/bin/micromamba';

export MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX='/root/.local/share/mamba';

__mamba_setup="$("$MAMBA_EXE" shell hook --shell bash --root-prefix "$MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX" 2> /dev/null)"

if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then

    eval "$__mamba_setup"

else

    alias micromamba="$MAMBA_EXE"  # Fallback on help from micromamba activate

fi

unset __mamba_setup

# <<< mamba initialize <<<

Running `shell init`, which:

 - modifies RC file: "/root/.bashrc"

 - generates config for root prefix: [1m"/root/.local/share/mamba"[0m

 - sets mamba executable to: [1m"/usr/local/bin/micromamba"[0m

The following has been added in your "/root/.bashrc" file



# >>> mamba initialize >>>

# !! Contents within this block are managed by 'micromamba shell init' !!

export MAMBA_EXE='/usr/local/bin/micromamba';

export MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX='/root/.local/share/mamba';

__mamba_setup="$("$MAMBA_EXE" shell hook --shell bash --root-prefix "$MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX" 2> /dev/null)"

if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then

    eval "$__mamba_setup"

else

    alias micromamba="$MAMBA_EXE"  # Fallback on help from micromamba activate

fi

unset __mamba_setup

# <<< mamba initialize <<<

Running `shell init`, which:

 - modifies RC file: "/root/.bashrc"

The following has been added in your "/root/.bashrc" file



# >>> mamba initialize >>>

# !! Contents within this block are managed by 'micromamba shell init' !!

export MAMBA_EXE='/usr/local/bin/micromamba';

export MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX='/root/.local/share/mamba';

__mamba_setup="$("$MAMBA_EXE" shell hook --shell bash --root-prefix "$MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX" 2> /dev/null)"

if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then

    eval "$__mamba_setup"

else

    alias micromamba="$MAMBA_EXE"  # Fallback on help from micromamba activate

fi

unset __mamba_setup

# <<< mamba initialize <<<

# >>> mamba initialize >>>

# !! Contents within this block are managed by 'micromamba shell init' !!

export MAMBA_EXE='/usr/local/bin/micromamba';

export MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX='/root/.local/share/mamba';

__mamba_setup="$("$MAMBA_EXE" shell hook --shell bash --root-prefix "$MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX" 2> /dev/null)"

if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then

    eval "$__mamba_setup"

else

    alias micromamba="$MAMBA_EXE"  # Fallback on help from micromamba activate

fi

unset __mamba_setup

=== Setting up micromamba environment ===

Running `shell init`, which:

 - modifies RC file: "/root/.bashrc"

 - generates config for root prefix: [1m"/root/.local/share/mamba"[0m

 - sets mamba executable to: [1m"/usr/local/bin/micromamba"[0m

The following has been added in your "/root/.bashrc" file



# >>> mamba initialize >>>

# !! Contents within this block are managed by 'micromamba shell init' !!

export MAMBA_EXE='/usr/local/bin/micromamba';

export MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX='/root/.local/share/mamba';

__mamba_setup="$("$MAMBA_EXE" shell hook --shell bash --root-prefix "$MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX" 2> /dev/null)"

if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then

    eval "$__mamba_setup"

else

    alias micromamba="$MAMBA_EXE"  # Fallback on help from micromamba activate

fi

unset __mamba_setup

# <<< mamba initialize <<<

# >>> mamba initialize >>>

# !! Contents within this block are managed by 'micromamba shell init' !!

export MAMBA_EXE='/openhands/micromamba/bin/micromamba';

export MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX='/home/openhands/.local/share/mamba';

__mamba_setup="$("$MAMBA_EXE" shell hook --shell bash --root-prefix "$MAMBA_ROOT_PREFIX" 2> /dev/null)"

if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then

    eval "$__mamba_setup"

else

    alias micromamba="$MAMBA_EXE"  # Fallback on help from micromamba activate

fi

unset __mamba_setup

# <<< mamba initialize <<<
